If a user clicks a toggle filter (e.g., Hide Auto Screenshots) while in Timeline View, the React list simply filters out those items.\n5. The editor remains the single source of truth. All filtering, sorting, searching, and navigation operate on metadata indexes and derived views.\n\n## Core Principles\n\n### Rule 1 — Editor Is Sacred\nThe editor content must never be automatically reordered, regrouped, rewritten, reassigned, or moved. User-created note structure is preserved exactly as written.\n\n### Rule 2 — Metadata Is Permanent\nEvery inserted item must contain structured metadata:\n- **Marker:** `<div data-type=\"marker\" data-timestamp=\"12\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Manual Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-source=\"manual\" data-timestamp=\"18\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Auto Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-source=\"auto\" data-timestamp=\"24\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\nMetadata becomes the source of truth. No inference from styling or DOM position.\n\n## Toolbar Addition\nInsert a new control exactly between `Marker` and `H A P`:\n`Marker | Filter & Organize ▼ | H | A | P`\nUse the Sliders icon from Lucide matching the existing toolbar styling. No emojis.\n\n## Dropdown Structure\n**VISIBILITY**\n☑ Show Markers\n☑ Show Manual Screenshots\n☑ Show Auto Screenshots\n\n**ORGANIZATION**\n☑ Timeline View\n\n**QUICK ACTIONS**\n- Show All (restores all visibility filters)\n- Hide All (hides markers and screenshots while preserving text content)\n\n## Visibility Engine\nFiltering must be visual only. Never delete elements, modify HTML, mutate stored data, or rebuild editor content.\n\n### CSS Filtering System\nApply classes (`.hide-markers`, `.hide-manual-screenshots`, `.hide-auto-screenshots`) and use CSS rules:\n```css\n.hide-markers [data-type=\"marker\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-manual-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"manual\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-auto-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"auto\"] { display: none !important; }\n```\nBenefits: Instant updates, export safe, sync safe, undo safe, cloud safe.\n\n## Metadata Index System\nDo NOT parse the entire editor every time Timeline View is opened. Instead, create a lightweight index:\n```ts\ninterface TimelineIndexItem {\n  id: string;\n  documentId: string;\n  videoId: string;\n  videoTitle: string;\n  timestamp: number;\n  createdAt?: number;\n  type: 'marker' | 'screenshot';\n  source?: 'manual' | 'auto';\n  originalElementId: string;\n  searchText?: string;\n}\n```\n\n### Index Lifecycle\nUpdate the index ONLY when:\n- Marker inserted\n- Screenshot inserted\n- Marker deleted\n- Screenshot deleted\n- Document loaded\nNever rebuild on every render. Never scan the editor unnecessarily.\n\n## Timeline View Architecture\nTimeline View is a derived interface. It is NOT editor sorting. The editor never changes.\n\n### Timeline Generation & Navigation\nWhen Timeline View is enabled:\n1. Read the `TimelineIndex`.\n2. Create a sorted copy by timestamp.\n3. Render Timeline UI as a clean chronological feed.\n4. The editor remains hidden underneath and HTML untouched.\n\nEvery TimelineItem maintains `originalElementId`. When clicked:\n1. Exit Timeline View.\n2. Scroll editor to original element.\n3. Briefly highlight the target.\n4. Restore focus nearby.\nTimeline View acts as a navigation layer, not an editor.\n\n## Search-Ready Architecture & Future Compatibility\n- Prepare for future global search by storing `searchText` inside `TimelineIndexItem`.\n- Must remain compatible with Google Drive sync, Android/iOS apps, Folder systems, Search systems, Export engine, and Cloud backups. No schema changes should be required later.\n\n## State Persistence\nPersist `showMarkers`, `showManualScreenshots`, `showAutoScreenshots`, and `timelineViewEnabled` inside settings storage. Incorporating the 10/10 refinements: runtime-only indexing, extended future types, and soft-delete support.","UserFacing":true},"CodeContent":"# Implementation Plan: Filter, Organize & Knowledge Index System V6 (Final 10/10 Architecture)\n\nThis is the definitive, production-ready architecture for NullNote's knowledge layer. It transforms the editor into an immutable source of truth and establishes a purely derived, runtime-only indexing layer that powers all current and future capabilities (Timeline View, Search, Analytics, Mobile Apps, Google Drive Sync).\n\n## Core Principles\n\n### Rule 1 — Editor Is Sacred (The Only Source of Truth)\nThe editor content is authoritative. It must never be automatically reordered, regrouped, rewritten, reassigned, or relocated. User-created note structure must remain exactly as written. No feature may modify the editor automatically.\n\n### Rule 2 — Knowledge Index is Runtime Only\nThe Knowledge Index is a **derived runtime structure**. It must never be persisted to storage or become a second source of truth to avoid duplicate data, sync conflicts, and corruption risks. The index is entirely rebuilt in memory whenever a document is loaded, ensuring absolute fidelity to the editor's DOM.\n\n### Rule 3 — Metadata Is Permanent\nEvery inserted content block must contain structured metadata:\n- **Marker:** `<div data-type=\"marker\" data-timestamp=\"12\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Manual Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-source=\"manual\" data-timestamp=\"18\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Auto Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-source=\"auto\" data-timestamp=\"24\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\nMetadata within the HTML is the permanent source of truth. Never infer content type from styling or DOM position.\n\n## Toolbar Addition\nInsert a new control exactly between `Marker` and `H A P`:\n`Marker | Filter & Organize ▼ | H | A | P`\nUse the Lucide `SlidersHorizontal` icon, maintaining existing toolbar styling and hover states. No emojis.\n\n## Dropdown Structure\n**VISIBILITY**\n☑ Markers (12)\n☑ Manual Screenshots (25)\n☑ Auto Screenshots (73)\n*(Counts update dynamically)*\n\n**ORGANIZATION**\n☑ Timeline View\n*(Future-proofed for Activity View, Search View, Folder View)*\n\n**QUICK ACTIONS**\n- Show All (restores visibility)\n- Hide All (hides markers and screenshots while preserving note text)\n\n## Visibility Engine\nFiltering is visual only using CSS. Never delete content, modify editor HTML, or rebuild editor structure.\n\n### CSS Filtering System\nApply classes (`.hide-markers`, `.hide-manual-screenshots`, `.hide-auto-screenshots`) and use CSS rules:\n```css\n.hide-markers [data-type=\"marker\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-manual-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"manual\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-auto-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"auto\"] { display: none !important; }\n```\nBenefits: O(1) updates, export safe, sync safe, undo safe, cloud safe.\n\n## Knowledge Index Architecture\nA purely in-memory, runtime index that powers Timeline View, Search, Mobile Apps, Google Drive Sync, Analytics, Folder System, and Export Intelligence.\n\n### Knowledge Item Model\n```ts\ninterface KnowledgeItem {\n  id: string;\n  documentId: string;\n  videoId: string;\n  videoTitle: string;\n  timestamp: number;\n  createdAt: number;\n  \n  // Future-proofed content types\n  type: \"marker\" | \"screenshot\" | \"note\" | \"bookmark\" | \"attachment\";\n  source?: \"manual\" | \"auto\";\n  \n  originalElementId: string;\n  searchText?: string;\n  thumbnail?: string;\n  \n  // Future-proofed soft delete support (Undo/Analytics/Sync)\n  isDeleted?: boolean; \n}\n```\n\n### Knowledge Index Lifecycle\n- Built entirely into memory upon **Document Load**.\n- Updated dynamically in memory ONLY when a marker/screenshot is inserted or deleted.\n- Destroyed when the document is closed.\nNever rebuild on every render. Never parse the entire editor repeatedly.\n\n## Timeline View Architecture\nTimeline View is a derived interface. It is NOT editor sorting. The editor never changes.\n\n### Timeline Generation & Navigation\nWhen Timeline View is enabled:\n1. Read the runtime Knowledge Index.\n2. Create a sorted copy by timestamp.\n3. Render Timeline UI. The editor remains hidden underneath and HTML untouched.\n\nEvery KnowledgeItem maintains `originalElementId`. When clicked:\n1. Exit Timeline View.\n2. Scroll to the original editor element.\n3. Highlight briefly.\n4. Restore focus.\nTimeline acts as a navigation layer, not a second editor.\n\n## Search-Ready & Future Architecture\n- **Search:** Store `searchText` in the Knowledge Index to power future search across markers, screenshots, notes, folders, and synced content.\n- **Folders:** Prepare for deep categorization without schema changes.\n- **Mobile/Drive Support:** The Android/iOS apps and Google Drive sync will consume this structured Knowledge Index directly for instant load times and conflict resolution.\n\n## State Persistence\nPersist `showMarkers`, `showManualScreenshots`, `showAutoScreenshots`, and `timelineViewEnabled` in settings storage. Must survive reloads, browser restarts, and updates.\n\n## Verification Plan\n1. **Visibility:** Toggle filters and verify instant visual hiding while storage and exports remain intact.\n2. **Timeline Ordering:** Verify items render chronologically in the Timeline without altering the editor's DOM.\n3. **Navigation:** Click a timeline item to verify scroll, highlight, and focus restoration.\n4. **Counts:** Ensure dropdown badges (e.g., Markers (12)) always match actual content.\n5. **Persistence & Regression:** Verify settings restore after reload, and ensure standard operations (notes, exports, undo/redo) function flawlessly.","Description":"Updating the implementation plan to the final V6 10/10 Architecture based on user feedback.","Overwrite":true,"TargetFile":"/Users/iamsparsh00321/.gemini/antigravity/brain/ebf4a875-5e0f-4e8f-ba02-c80ade1a9232/implementation_plan.md","toolAction":"Update plan","toolSummary":"Update to V6 Plan"}}]}

It transforms the editor into an immutable source of truth and establishes a purely derived, runtime-only indexing layer that powers all current and future capabilities (Timeline View, Search, Analytics).\n\n## Core Principles\n\n### Rule 1 — Editor Is Sacred (The Only Source of Truth)\nThe editor content is authoritative. It must never be automatically reordered, regrouped, rewritten, reassigned, or relocated. User-created note structure must remain exactly as written. No feature may modify the editor automatically.\n\n### Rule 2 — Knowledge Index is a Runtime Projection\nThe Knowledge Index is a **derived runtime structure**. It is never persisted as an independent source of truth to avoid duplicate data, sync conflicts, and corruption risks. The index is entirely rebuilt in memory whenever a document is loaded. **External systems (Search, Mobile, Drive, Analytics) must generate their own Knowledge Index from the underlying document data.**\n\n### Rule 3 — Metadata Is Permanent & Versioned\nEvery inserted content block must contain structured, versioned metadata:\n- **Marker:** `<div data-type=\"marker\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-timestamp=\"12\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Manual Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-source=\"manual\" data-timestamp=\"18\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\n- **Auto Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-source=\"auto\" data-timestamp=\"24\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"...\">`\nMetadata within the HTML is the permanent source of truth. The schema version ensures painless future migrations (v2, v3, etc.). Never infer content type from styling or DOM position.\n\n## Toolbar Addition\nInsert a new control exactly between `Marker` and `H A P`:\n`Marker | Filter & Organize ▼ | H | A | P`\nUse the Lucide `SlidersHorizontal` icon, maintaining existing toolbar styling and hover states. No emojis.\n\n## Dropdown Structure\n**VISIBILITY**\n☑ Markers (12)\n☑ Manual Screenshots (25)\n☑ Auto Screenshots (73)\n*(Counts update dynamically)*\n\n**ORGANIZATION**\n☑ Timeline View\n*(Future-proofed for Activity View, Search View, Folder View)*\n\n**QUICK ACTIONS**\n- Show All (restores visibility)\n- Hide All (hides markers and screenshots while preserving note text)\n\n## Visibility Engine\nFiltering is visual only using CSS. Never delete content, modify editor HTML, or rebuild editor structure.\n\n### CSS Filtering System\nApply classes (`.hide-markers`, `.hide-manual-screenshots`, `.hide-auto-screenshots`) and use CSS rules:\n```css\n.hide-markers [data-type=\"marker\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-manual-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"manual\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-auto-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"auto\"] { display: none !important; }\n```\nBenefits: O(1) updates, export safe, sync safe, undo safe, cloud safe.\n\n## Knowledge Index Architecture\nA purely in-memory, runtime index that powers Timeline View, Search, Analytics, Folder System, and Export Intelligence.\n\n### Knowledge Item Model\n```ts\ninterface KnowledgeItem {\n  id: string;\n  documentId: string;\n  videoId: string;\n  videoTitle: string;\n  timestamp: number;\n  createdAt: number;\n  updatedAt?: number; // Crucial for Drive Sync, Conflict Resolution, & Recent Activity\n  \n  // Future-proofed content types\n  type: \"marker\" | \"screenshot\" | \"note\" | \"bookmark\" | \"attachment\";\n  source?: \"manual\" | \"auto\";\n  \n  originalElementId: string;\n  searchText?: string;\n  thumbnail?: string;\n  \n  // Future-proofed soft delete support (Undo/Analytics/Sync)\n  isDeleted?: boolean; \n}\n```\n\n### Knowledge Index Lifecycle\n- Built entirely into memory upon **Document Load**.\n- Updated dynamically in memory ONLY when a marker/screenshot is inserted or deleted.\n- Destroyed when the document is closed.\nNever rebuild on every render. Never parse the entire editor repeatedly.\n\n## Timeline View Architecture\nTimeline View is a derived interface. It is NOT editor sorting. The editor never changes.\n\n### Timeline Generation & Navigation\nWhen Timeline View is enabled:\n1. Read the runtime Knowledge Index.\n2. Create a sorted copy by timestamp.\n3. Render Timeline UI. The editor remains hidden underneath and HTML untouched.\n\nEvery KnowledgeItem maintains `originalElementId`. When clicked:\n1. Exit Timeline View.\n2. Scroll to the original editor element.\n3. Highlight briefly.\n4. Restore focus.\nTimeline acts as a navigation layer, not a second editor.\n\n## State Persistence\nPersist `showMarkers`, `showManualScreenshots`, `showAutoScreenshots`, and `timelineViewEnabled` in settings storage. It transforms the editor into an immutable source of truth and establishes a purely derived, runtime-only indexing layer that powers all current and future capabilities (Timeline View, Search, Analytics).\n\n## Core Principles\n\n### Rule 1 — Editor Is Sacred (The Only Source of Truth)\nThe editor content is authoritative. It must never be automatically reordered, regrouped, rewritten, reassigned, or relocated. User-created note structure must remain exactly as written. No feature may modify the editor automatically.\n\n### Rule 2 — Knowledge Index is a Runtime Projection\nThe Knowledge Index is a **derived runtime structure**. It is never persisted as an independent source of truth to avoid duplicate data, sync conflicts, and corruption risks. The index is entirely rebuilt in memory whenever a document is loaded. **External systems (Search, Mobile, Drive, Analytics) must generate their own Knowledge Index from the underlying document data.**\n\n### Rule 3 — Metadata Is Permanent, Versioned, & Globally Unique\nEvery inserted content block must contain structured, versioned, and uniquely identifiable metadata:\n- **Marker:** `<div data-type=\"marker\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-timestamp=\"12\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"[UUID]\">`\n- **Manual Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-source=\"manual\" data-timestamp=\"18\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"[UUID]\">`\n- **Auto Screenshot:** `<div data-type=\"screenshot\" data-schema-version=\"1\" data-source=\"auto\" data-timestamp=\"24\" data-document-id=\"...\" data-video-id=\"...\" data-element-id=\"[UUID]\">`\n\n**UUID Rule:** Every marker and screenshot element must receive a globally unique identifier (`crypto.randomUUID()`). IDs must never be reused and must remain stable across save/load cycles. Timeline navigation and future sync rely on these identifiers.\n\n## Toolbar Addition\nInsert a new control exactly between `Marker` and `H A P`:\n`Marker | Filter & Organize ▼ | H | A | P`\nUse the Lucide `SlidersHorizontal` icon, maintaining existing toolbar styling and hover states. No emojis.\n\n## Dropdown Structure\n**VISIBILITY**\n☑ Markers (12)\n☑ Manual Screenshots (25)\n☑ Auto Screenshots (73)\n*(Counts update dynamically)*\n\n**ORGANIZATION**\n☑ Timeline View\n*(Future-proofed for Activity View, Search View, Folder View)*\n\n**QUICK ACTIONS**\n- Show All (restores visibility)\n- Hide All (hides markers and screenshots while preserving note text)\n\n## Visibility Engine\nFiltering is visual only using CSS. Never delete content, modify editor HTML, or rebuild editor structure.\n\n### CSS Filtering System\nApply classes (`.hide-markers`, `.hide-manual-screenshots`, `.hide-auto-screenshots`) and use CSS rules:\n```css\n.hide-markers [data-type=\"marker\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-manual-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"manual\"] { display: none !important; }\n.hide-auto-screenshots [data-type=\"screenshot\"][data-source=\"auto\"] { display: none !important; }\n```\nBenefits: O(1) updates, export safe, sync safe, undo safe, cloud safe.\n\n## Knowledge Index Architecture\nA purely in-memory, runtime index that powers Timeline View, Search, Analytics, Folder System, and Export Intelligence.\n\n### Knowledge Item Model\n```ts\ninterface KnowledgeItem {\n  id: string; // The globally unique data-element-id\n  documentId: string;\n  videoId: string;\n  videoTitle: string;\n  timestamp: number;\n  createdAt: number;\n  updatedAt?: number; // Crucial for Drive Sync, Conflict Resolution, & Recent Activity\n  \n  // Future-proofed content types\n  type: \"marker\" | \"screenshot\" | \"note\" | \"bookmark\" | \"attachment\";\n  source?: \"manual\" | \"auto\";\n  \n  originalElementId: string; // Maps back to the exact DOM element\n  searchText?: string;\n  thumbnail?: string;\n  \n  // Future-proofed soft delete support (Undo/Analytics/Sync)\n  isDeleted?: boolean; \n}\n```\n\n### Knowledge Index Lifecycle\n- Built entirely into memory upon **Document Load**.\n- Updated dynamically in memory ONLY when a marker/screenshot is inserted or deleted.\n- Destroyed when the document is closed.\nNever rebuild on every render. Never parse the entire editor repeatedly.\n\n## Timeline View Architecture\nTimeline View is a derived interface. It is NOT editor sorting. The editor never changes.\n\n### Timeline Generation & Navigation\nWhen Timeline View is enabled:\n1. Read the runtime Knowledge Index.\n2. Create a sorted copy by timestamp.\n3. Render Timeline UI. The editor remains hidden underneath and HTML untouched.\n\nEvery KnowledgeItem maintains `originalElementId`. When clicked:\n1. Exit Timeline View.\n2. Scroll to the original editor element.\n3. Highlight briefly.\n4. Restore focus.\nTimeline acts as a navigation layer, not a second editor.\n\n## State Persistence\n**Filters are global, Timeline is temporary.**\nPersist `showMarkers`, `showManualScreenshots`, and `showAutoScreenshots` in settings storage so user preferences survive reloads.\n**DO NOT** persist `timelineViewEnabled`. maxHeight) {\\n84:     height = maxHeight;\\n85:     width = height * ratio;\\n86:   }\\n87:   if (width > maxWidth) {\\n88:     width = maxWidth;\\n89:     height = width / ratio;\\n90:   }\\n91: \\n92:   return {\\n93:     width: Math.round(width),\\n94:     height: Math.round(height),\\n95:   };\\n96: }\\n97: \\n98: // ─── Block Measurement ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\n99: \\n100: /**\\n101:  * Measure the height a text block will require.\\n102:  * Uses approximate character-per-line calculation.\\n103:  */\\n104: function measureTextBlock(text: string): number {\\n105:   const fontSize = PDF_FONT.BODY_SIZE;\\n106:   const lineHeight = fontSize * PDF_FONT.BODY_LINE_HEIGHT;\\n107:   const charsPerLine = Math.floor(PDF_CONTENT.WIDTH / (fontSize * 0.5));\\n108:   const lineCount = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(text.length / charsPerLine));\\n109:   return lineCount * lineHeight + PDF_SPACING.AFTER_TEXT;\\n110: }\\n111: \\n112: /**\\n113:  * Measure a timestamp line height.\\n114:  */\\n115: function measureTimestampLine(): number {\\n116:   return PDF_FONT.TIMESTAMP_SIZE + PDF_SPACING.BEFORE_TIMESTAMP + PDF_SPACING.AFTER_TIMESTAMP;\\n117: }\\n118: \\n119: /**\\n120:  * Measure all blocks and return them with their required heights.\\n121:  */\\n122: export function measureBlocks(\\n123:   doc: ExportDocument,\\n124:   maxWidth: number = PDF_CONTENT.WIDTH,\\n125:   maxImageHeight: number = PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT * 0.7\\n126: ): MeasuredBlock[] {\\n127:   return doc.blocks.map((block) => {\\n128:     let requiredHeight = 0;\\n129:     let imageWidth: number | undefined;\\n130:     let imageHeight: number | undefined;\\n131: \\n132:     switch (block.type) {\\n133:       case 'text': {\\n134:         requiredHeight = measureTextBlock(block.text || '');\\n135:         break;\\n136:       }\\n137: \\n138:       case 'marker': {\\n139:         // Timestamp line\\n140:         requiredHeight += measureTimestampLine();\\n141: \\n142:         // Optional screenshot\\n143:         if (block.hasScreenshot && block.screenshotData) {\\n144:           const dims = calculateImageDimensions(\\n145:             block.screenshotWidth || 0,\\n146:             block.screenshotHeight || 0,\\n147:             maxWidth,\\n148:             maxImageHeight\\n149:           );\\n150:           imageWidth = dims.width;\\n151:           imageHeight = dims.height;\\n152:           requiredHeight += dims.height + PDF_SPACING.AFTER_IMAGE;\\n153:         }\\n154:         break;\\n155:       }\\n156: \\n157:       case 'screenshot': {\\n158:         // Timestamp line\\n159:         requiredHeight += measureTimestampLine();\\n160: \\n161:         // Screenshot image\\n162:         if (block.screenshotData) {\\n163:           const dims = calculateImageDimensions(\\n164:             block.screenshotWidth || 0,\\n165:             block.screenshotHeight || 0,\\n166:             maxWidth,\\n167:             maxImageHeight\\n168:           );\\n169:           imageWidth = dims.width;\\n170:           imageHeight = dims.height;\\n171:           requiredHeight += dims.height + PDF_SPACING.AFTER_IMAGE;\\n172:         }\\n173:         break;\\n174:       }\\n175:     }\\n176: \\n177:     return {\\n178:       block,\\n179:       requiredHeight,\\n180:       imageWidth,\\n181:       imageHeight,\\n182:     };\\n183:   });\\n184: }\\n185: \\n186: // ─── Header Measurement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\n187: \\n188: /**\\n189:  * Calculate the total height consumed by the header area on page 1.\\n190:  * Includes: branding row, separator, title, URL, spacing.\\n191:  */\\n192: export function measureHeader(doc: ExportDocument): number {\\n193:   let height = 0;\\n194: \\n195:   // Branding row: logo + text\\n196:   height += PDF_LOGO.HEIGHT;\\n197:   height += PDF_SPACING.HEADER_LINE_OFFSET;\\n198: \\n199:   // Separator line (thin but needs spacing)\\n200:   height += 1;\\n201:   height += PDF_SPACING.AFTER_HEADER;\\n202: \\n203:   // Title\\n204:   height += PDF_FONT.TITLE_SIZE * 1.3; // line height\\n205: \\n206:   // URL (if present)\\n207:   if (doc.videoUrl) {\\n208:     height += 6; // gap between title and URL\\n209:     height += PDF_FONT.URL_SIZE * 1.4;\\n210:   }\\n211: \\n212:   // Space after title block\\n213:   height += PDF_SPACING.AFTER_TITLE_BLOCK;\\n214: \\n215:   return height;\\n216: }\\n217: \\n218: // ─── Pagination Engine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\n219: \\n220: /**\\n221:  * Assign measured blocks to pages.\\n222:  *\\n223:  * Algorithm:\\n224:  * 1. Page 1 starts with reduced available height (header area)\\n225:  * 2. For each block, check if it fits in remaining space\\n226:  * 3. If it doesn't fit → start a new page\\n227:  * 4. Never split a block across pages\\n228:  *\\n229:  * This guarantees:\\n230:  * - No blank pages (we only create a page when there's content for it)\\n231:  * - No split images\\n232:  * - Deterministic layout regardless of viewport\\n233:  */\\n234: export function paginate(\\n235:   doc: ExportDocument,\\n236:   measuredBlocks: MeasuredBlock[]\\n237: ): PageLayout[] {\\n238:   const pages: PageLayout[] = [];\\n239:   let currentPage: PageLayout = { pageNumber: 1, blocks: [] };\\n240:   pages.push(currentPage);\\n241: \\n242:   // Page 1 has less available space due to header\\n243:   const headerHeight = measureHeader(doc);\\n244:   let remainingHeight = PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT - headerHeight;\\n245: \\n246:   for (const mb of measuredBlocks) {\\n247:     if (mb.requiredHeight <= 0) continue; // skip empty blocks\\n248: \\n249:     if (mb.requiredHeight > remainingHeight) {\\n250:       // Block doesn't fit on current page\\n251:       // Only create a new page if current page has content\\n252:       // (prevents blank pages)\\n253:       if (currentPage.blocks.length > 0) {\\n254:         currentPage = {\\n255:           pageNumber: pages.length + 1,\\n256:           blocks: [],\\n257:         };\\n258:         pages.push(currentPage);\\n259:         remainingHeight = PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT;\\n260:       }\\n261: \\n262:       // If a single block is taller than a full page, we still place it\\n263:       // (it will overflow but won't create a blank page)\\n264:       if (mb.requiredHeight > PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT) {\\n265:         // Scale down oversized images to fit one page\\n266:         if (mb.imageHeight && mb.imageHeight > PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT * 0.8) {\\n267:           const scale = (PDF_CONTENT.HEIGHT * 0.7) / mb.imageHeight;\\n268:           mb.imageHeight = Math.round(mb.imageHeight * scale);\\n269:           mb.imageWidth = mb.imageWidth ? Math.round(mb.imageWidth * scale) : undefined;\\n270:           mb.requiredHeight = measureTimestampLine() + mb.imageHeight + PDF_SPACING.AFTER_IMAGE;\\n271:         }\\n272:       }\\n273:     }\\n274: \\n275:     currentPage.blocks.push(mb);\\n276:     remainingHeight -= mb.requiredHeight;\\n277:   }\\n278: \\n279:   // Remove any trailing empty pages (safety net)\\n280:   while (pages.length > 1 && pages[pages.length - 1].blocks.length === 0) {\\n281:     pages.pop();\\n282:   }\\n283: \\n284:   return pages;\\n285: }\\n286: \\n287: /**\\n288:  * Full layout pipeline: measure → paginate.\\n289:  */\\n290: export function layoutDocument(doc: ExportDocument): PageLayout[] {\\n291:   const measured = measureBlocks(doc);\\n292:   return paginate(doc, measured);\\n293: }\\n294: \\nThe above content shows the entire, complete file contents of the requested file.\\n\"}\n\n"}
